   162	// GetFullIdentifier returns the task identifier if the task has one and the index prefixed with # otherwise.
   163	func (t *Task) GetFullIdentifier() string {
   164	        if t.Identifier != "" {
   165	                if strings.HasPrefix(t.Identifier, "-") {
   166	                        return "#" + strings.TrimPrefix(t.Identifier, "-")
   167	                }
   168	                return t.Identifier
   169	        }
   170	
   171	        return "#" + strconv.FormatInt(t.Index, 10)
   172	}

   768	func checkBucketLimit(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, t *Task, bucket *Bucket) (taskCount int64, err error) {
   769	        view, err := GetProjectViewByID(s, bucket.ProjectViewID)
   770	        if err != nil {
   771	                return 0, err
   772	        }

   777	                        ProjectViewID: bucket.ProjectViewID,

   782	                        return 0, err
   783	                }

   801	func calculateDefaultPosition(entityID int64, position float64) float64 {
   802	        if position == 0 {
   803	                return float64(entityID) * math.Pow(2, 16)
   804	        }

   809	func calculateNextTaskIndex(s *xorm.Session, projectID int64) (nextIndex int64, err error) {
   810	        latestTask := &Task{}
   811	        _, err = s.
   812	                Where("project_id = ?", projectID).

   816	                return 0, err

   822	func setNewTaskIndex(s *xorm.Session, t *Task) (err error) {
   823	        // Check if an index was provided, otherwise calculate a new one
   824	        if t.Index == 0 {
   825	                t.Index, err = calculateNextTaskIndex(s, t.ProjectID)
   826	                return
   827	        }
   828	
   829	        // Check if the provided index is already taken
   830	        exists, err := s.Where("project_id = ? AND `index` = ?", t.ProjectID, t.Index).Exist(&Task{})
   831	        if err != nil {
   832	                return err
   833	        }
   834	        if exists {
   835	                // If the index is taken, calculate a new one
   836	                t.Index, err = calculateNextTaskIndex(s, t.ProjectID)
   837	                if err != nil {
   838	                        return err
   839	                }
   840	        }
   841	
   842	        return
   843	}

   969	func setTaskInBucketInViews(s *xorm.Session, t *Task, a web.Auth, setBucket bool, providedBucket *Bucket) ([]*TaskPosition, []*TaskBucket, error) {

   973	        }

   993	                                        }
   994	                                }
   995	                        }

  1009	                                }

  1012	
  1013	                                continue
  1014	                        }
  1015	
  1016	                        taskBuckets = append(taskBuckets, &TaskBucket{
  1017	                                BucketID:      bucketID,

  1033	        }
  1034

  1457	func addOneMonthToDate(d time.Time) time.Time {
  1458	        return time.Date(d.Year(), d.Month()+1, d.Day(), d.Hour(), d.Minute(), d.Second(), d.Nanosecond(), config.GetTimeZone())

  1461	func addRepeatIntervalToTime(now, t time.Time, duration time.Duration) time.Time {
  1462	        for {
  1463	                t = t.Add(duration)
  1464	                if t.After(now) {
  1465	                        break
  1466	                }
  1467	        }
  1468	
  1469	        return t

  1472	func setTaskDatesDefault(oldTask, newTask *Task) {
  1473	        if oldTask.RepeatAfter == 0 {
  1474	                return
  1475	        }
  1476	
  1477	        // Current time in an extra variable to base all calculations on the same time
  1478	        now := time.Now()
  1479	
  1480	        repeatDuration := time.Duration(oldTask.RepeatAfter) * time.Second
  1481	
  1482	        // assuming we'll merge the new task over the old task
  1483	        if !oldTask.DueDate.IsZero() {
  1484	                newTask.DueDate = addRepeatIntervalToTime(now, oldTask.DueDate, repeatDuration)
  1485	        }
  1486	
  1487	        newTask.Reminders = oldTask.Reminders
  1488	        // When repeating from the current date, all reminders should keep their difference to each other.
  1489	        // To make this easier, we sort them first because we can then rely on the fact the first is the smallest
  1490	        if len(oldTask.Reminders) > 0 {
  1491	                for in, r := range oldTask.Reminders {
  1492	                        newTask.Reminders[in].Reminder = addRepeatIntervalToTime(now, r.Reminder, repeatDuration)
  1493	                }
  1494	        }
  1495	
  1496	        // If a task has a start and end date, the end date should keep the difference to the start date when setting them as new
  1497	        if !oldTask.StartDate.IsZero() {
  1498	                newTask.StartDate = addRepeatIntervalToTime(now, oldTask.StartDate, repeatDuration)
  1499	        }
  1500	
  1501	        if !oldTask.EndDate.IsZero() {
  1502	                newTask.EndDate = addRepeatIntervalToTime(now, oldTask.EndDate, repeatDuration)
  1503	        }
  1504	
  1505	        newTask.Done = false
  1506	}

  1537	func setTaskDatesFromCurrentDateRepeat(oldTask, newTask *Task) {
  1538	        if oldTask.RepeatAfter == 0 {
  1539	                return
  1540	        }
  1541	
  1542	        // Current time in an extra variable to base all calculations on the same time
  1543	        now := time.Now()
  1544	
  1545	        repeatDuration := time.Duration(oldTask.RepeatAfter) * time.Second
  1546	
  1547	        // assuming we'll merge the new task over the old task
  1548	        if !oldTask.DueDate.IsZero() {
  1549	                newTask.DueDate = now.Add(repeatDuration)
  1550	        }
  1551	
  1552	        newTask.Reminders = oldTask.Reminders
  1553	        // When repeating from the current date, all reminders should keep their difference to each other.
  1554	        // To make this easier, we sort them first because we can then rely on the fact the first is the smallest
  1555	        if len(oldTask.Reminders) > 0 {
  1556	                sort.Slice(oldTask.Reminders, func(i, j int) bool {
  1557	                        return oldTask.Reminders[i].Reminder.Unix() < oldTask.Reminders[j].Reminder.Unix()
  1558	                })
  1559	                first := oldTask.Reminders[0].Reminder
  1560	                for in, r := range oldTask.Reminders {
  1561	                        diff := r.Reminder.Sub(first)
  1562	                        newTask.Reminders[in].Reminder = now.Add(repeatDuration + diff)
  1563	                }
  1564	        }
  1565	
  1566	        // We want to preserve intervals among the due, start and end dates.
  1567	        // The due date is used as a reference point for all new dates, so the
  1568	        // behaviour depends on whether the due date is set at all.
  1569	        if oldTask.DueDate.IsZero() {
  1570	                // If a task has no due date, but does have a start and end date, the
  1571	                // end date should keep the difference to the start date when setting
  1572	                // them as new
  1573	                if !oldTask.StartDate.IsZero() && !oldTask.EndDate.IsZero() {
  1574	                        diff := oldTask.EndDate.Sub(oldTask.StartDate)
  1575	                        newTask.StartDate = now.Add(repeatDuration)
  1576	                        newTask.EndDate = now.Add(repeatDuration + diff)
  1577	                } else {
  1578	                        if !oldTask.StartDate.IsZero() {
  1579	                                newTask.StartDate = now.Add(repeatDuration)
  1580	                        }
  1581	
  1582	                        if !oldTask.EndDate.IsZero() {
  1583	                                newTask.EndDate = now.Add(repeatDuration)
  1584	                        }
  1585	                }
  1586	        } else {
  1587	                // If the old task has a start and due date, we set the new start date
  1588	                // to preserve the interval between them.
  1589	                if !oldTask.StartDate.IsZero() {
  1590	                        diff := oldTask.DueDate.Sub(oldTask.StartDate)
  1591	                        newTask.StartDate = newTask.DueDate.Add(-diff)
  1592	                }
  1593	
  1594	                // If the old task has an end and due date, we set the new end date
  1595	                // to preserve the interval between them.
  1596	                if !oldTask.EndDate.IsZero() {
  1597	                        diff := oldTask.DueDate.Sub(oldTask.EndDate)
  1598	                        newTask.EndDate = newTask.DueDate.Add(-diff)
  1599	                }
  1600	        }
  1601	
  1602	        newTask.Done = false
  1603	}
  1604	
  1605	// This helper function updates the reminders, doneAt, start, end and due dates of the *old* task
  1606	// and saves the new values in the newTask object.
  1607	// We make a few assumptions here:
  1608	//  1. Everything in oldTask is the truth - we figure out if we update anything at all if oldTask.RepeatAfter has a value > 0
  1609	//  2. Because of 1., this functions should not be used to update values other than Done in the same go
  1610	func updateDone(oldTask *Task, newTask *Task) (updateDoneAt bool) {
  1611	        // Track if the done status changed before repeat helpers modify it
  1612	        doneStatusChanged := oldTask.Done != newTask.Done
  1613	
  1614	        if !oldTask.Done && newTask.Done {
  1615	                switch oldTask.RepeatMode {
  1616	                case TaskRepeatModeMonth:
  1617	                        setTaskDatesMonthRepeat(oldTask, newTask)
  1618	                case TaskRepeatModeFromCurrentDate:
  1619	                        setTaskDatesFromCurrentDateRepeat(oldTask, newTask)
  1620	                case TaskRepeatModeDefault:
  1621	                        setTaskDatesDefault(oldTask, newTask)
  1622	                }
  1623	
  1624	                newTask.DoneAt = time.Now()
  1625	        }
  1626	
  1627	        // When unmarking a task as done, reset the timestamp
  1628	        if oldTask.Done && !newTask.Done {
  1629	                newTask.DoneAt = time.Time{}
  1630	        }
  1631	
  1632	        return doneStatusChanged
  1633	}
  1634	
  1635	// Set the absolute trigger dates for Reminders with relative period
  1636	func updateRelativeReminderDates(task *Task) (err error) {
  1637	        for _, reminder := range task.Reminders {
  1638	                relativeDuration := time.Duration(reminder.RelativePeriod) * time.Second
  1639	                if reminder.RelativeTo != "" {
  1640	                        reminder.Reminder = time.Time{}

    29	// TaskBucket represents the relation between a task and a kanban bucket.
    30	// A task can only appear once per project view which is ensured by a
    31	// unique index on the combination of task_id and project_view_id.
    32	type TaskBucket struct {
    33	        BucketID int64   `xorm:"bigint not null index" json:"bucket_id" param:"bucket"`
    34	        Bucket   *Bucket `xorm:"-" json:"bucket"`
    35	        // The task which belongs to the bucket. Together with ProjectViewID
    36	        // this field is part of a unique index to prevent duplicates.
    37	        TaskID int64 `xorm:"bigint not null index unique(task_view)" json:"task_id"`
    38	        // The view this bucket belongs to. Combined with TaskID this forms a
    39	        // unique index.
    40	        ProjectViewID int64 `xorm:"bigint not null index unique(task_view)" json:"project_view_id" param:"view"`
    41	        ProjectID     int64 `xorm:"-" json:"-" param:"project"`
    42	        Task          *Task `xorm:"-" json:"task"`
    43	
    44	        web.Permissions `xorm:"-" json:"-"`
    45	        web.CRUDable    `xorm:"-" json:"-"`
    46	}

    62	        count, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", b.TaskID, b.ProjectViewID).
    63	                Cols("bucket_id").

    66	                return
    67	        }

    86	// updateTaskBucket is internally used to actually do the update.
    87	func updateTaskBucket(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, b *TaskBucket) (err error) {
    88	        oldTaskBucket := &TaskBucket{}
    89	        _, err = s.
    90	                Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", b.TaskID, b.ProjectViewID).
    91	                Get(oldTaskBucket)
    92	        if err != nil {
    93	                return
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        if oldTaskBucket.BucketID == b.BucketID {
    97	                // no need to do anything
    98	                return
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        view, err := GetProjectViewByIDAndProject(s, b.ProjectViewID, b.ProjectID)
   102	        if err != nil {
   103	                return err
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        bucket, err := getBucketByID(s, b.BucketID)
   107	        if err != nil {
   108	                return err
   109	        }
   110	
   111	        // If there is a bucket set, make sure they belong to the same project as the task
   112	        if view.ID != bucket.ProjectViewID {
   113	                return ErrBucketDoesNotBelongToProjectView{
   114	                        ProjectViewID: view.ID,
   115	                        BucketID:      bucket.ID,
   116	                }
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        task := &Task{ID: b.TaskID}
   120	        err = task.ReadOne(s, a)
   121	        if err != nil {
   122	                return err
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        // Check the bucket limit
   126	        // Only check the bucket limit if the task is being moved between buckets, allow reordering the task within a bucket
   127	        if b.BucketID != 0 && b.BucketID != oldTaskBucket.BucketID {
   128	                taskCount, err := checkBucketLimit(s, a, task, bucket)
   129	                if err != nil {
   130	                        return err
   131	                }
   132	                bucket.Count = taskCount
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        var updateBucket = true
   136	
   137	        // mark task done if moved into or out of the done bucket
   138	        // Only change the done state if the task's done value actually changes
   139	        var doneChanged bool
   140	        if view.DoneBucketID != 0 {
   141	                if view.DoneBucketID == b.BucketID && !task.Done {
   142	                        doneChanged = true
   143	                        task.Done = true
   144	                        if task.isRepeating() {
   145	                                oldTask := *task
   146	                                oldTask.Done = false
   147	                                updateDone(&oldTask, task)
   148	                                updateBucket = false
   149	                                b.BucketID = oldTaskBucket.BucketID
   150	                        }
   151	                }
   152	
   153	                if oldTaskBucket.BucketID == view.DoneBucketID && task.Done && b.BucketID != view.DoneBucketID {
   154	                        doneChanged = true
   155	                        task.Done = false
   156	                }
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        if doneChanged {
   160	                if task.Done {
   161	                        task.DoneAt = time.Now()
   162	                } else {
   163	                        task.DoneAt = time.Time{}
   164	                }
   165	                _, err = s.Where("id = ?", task.ID).
   166	                        Cols(
   167	                                "done",
   168	                                "due_date",
   169	                                "start_date",
   170	                                "end_date",
   171	                                "done_at",
   172	                        ).
   173	                        Update(task)
   174	                if err != nil {
   175	                        return
   176	                }
   177	
   178	                err = task.updateReminders(s, task)
   179	                if err != nil {
   180	                        return
   181	                }
   182	
   183	                // Since the done state of the task was changed, we need to move the task into all done buckets everywhere
   184	                if task.Done {
   185	                        viewsWithDoneBucket := []*ProjectView{}
   186	                        err = s.
   187	                                Where("project_id = ? AND view_kind = ? AND bucket_configuration_mode = ? AND id != ? AND done_bucket_id != 0",
   188	                                        view.ProjectID, ProjectViewKindKanban, BucketConfigurationModeManual, view.ID).
   189	                                Find(&viewsWithDoneBucket)
   190	                        if err != nil {
   191	                                return
   192	                        }
   193	                        for _, v := range viewsWithDoneBucket {
   194	                                newBucket := &TaskBucket{
   195	                                        TaskID:        task.ID,
   196	                                        ProjectViewID: v.ID,
   197	                                        BucketID:      v.DoneBucketID,
   198	                                }
   199	                                err = newBucket.upsert(s)
   200	                                if err != nil {
   201	                                        return
   202	                                }
   203	                        }
   204	                }
   205	        }
   206	
   207	        if updateBucket {
   208	                err = b.upsert(s)
   209	                if err != nil {
   210	                        return
   211	                }
   212	                bucket.Count++
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        b.Task = task
   216	        b.Bucket = bucket
   217	
   218	        return
   219	}

   221	// Update is the handler to update a task bucket
   222	// @Summary Update a task bucket
   223	// @Description Updates a task in a bucket
   224	// @tags task
   225	// @Accept json

   235	// @Router /projects/{project}/views/{view}/buckets/{bucket}/tasks [post]
   236	func (b *TaskBucket) Update(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth) (err error) {
   237	        err = updateTaskBucket(s, a, b)
   238	        if err != nil {
   239	                return err
   240	        }

package repro_test

import (
    "testing"

    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/db"
    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/models"
    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/user"
)

func TestRecurringTaskMovedToDoneBucketGoesToDefaultBucket(t *testing.T) {
    models.SetupTests()
    user.InitTests()
    db.LoadAndAssertFixtures(t)

    s := db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()

    tb := &models.TaskBucket{
        TaskID:        28,
        BucketID:      3, // done bucket in view 4
        ProjectViewID: 4,
        ProjectID:     1,
    }
    if err := tb.Update(s, &user.User{ID: 1}); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("update bucket: %v", err)
    }
    if err := s.Commit(); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("commit: %v", err)
    }

    s = db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    stored := &models.TaskBucket{}
    has, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).Get(stored)
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("get task bucket: %v", err)
    }
    if !has {
        t.Fatalf("task bucket missing")
    }
    if stored.BucketID != 1 {
        t.Fatalf("expected recurring task to be in default bucket 1 after completion, got bucket %d", stored.BucketID)
    }
}
EOF

package repro_test

import (
    "testing"

    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/db"
    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/models"
    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/notifications"
    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/user"
)

func TestRecurringTaskMovedToDoneBucketGoesToDefaultBucket(t *testing.T) {
    user.InitTests()
    models.SetupTests()
    if err := db.InitTestFixtures(append([]string{
        "files", "label_tasks", "labels", "link_shares", "projects", "task_assignees", "task_attachments",
        "task_comments", "task_relations", "task_reminders", "tasks", "team_projects", "team_members", "teams",
        "users", "user_tokens", "users_projects", "buckets", "saved_filters", "subscriptions", "favorites",
        "api_tokens", "reactions", "project_views", "task_positions", "task_buckets", "sessions", "webhooks",
        "totp", "oauth_codes", "oauth_clients",
    }, notifications.GetTables()...)...); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("init fixtures: %v", err)
    }
    db.LoadAndAssertFixtures(t)

    s := db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()

    tb := &models.TaskBucket{
        TaskID:        28,
        BucketID:      3, // done bucket in view 4
        ProjectViewID: 4,
        ProjectID:     1,
    }
    if err := tb.Update(s, &user.User{ID: 1}); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("update bucket: %v", err)
    }
    if err := s.Commit(); err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("commit: %v", err)
    }

    s = db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    stored := &models.TaskBucket{}
    has, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).Get(stored)
    if err != nil {
        t.Fatalf("get task bucket: %v", err)
    }
    if !has {
        t.Fatalf("task bucket missing")
    }
    if stored.BucketID != 1 {
        t.Fatalf("expected recurring task to be in default bucket 1 after completion, got bucket %d", stored.BucketID)
    }
}

func TestReproRecurringTaskInDoingMovesToTodoAfterDone(t *testing.T) {
    db.LoadAndAssertFixtures(t)
    s := db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    u := &user.User{ID: 1}

    // Simulate the reproduction steps: recurring task is in Doing.
    _, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).
        Cols("bucket_id").
        Update(&TaskBucket{BucketID: 2})
    require.NoError(t, err)

    // User drags it to Done.
    tb := &TaskBucket{TaskID: 28, ProjectViewID: 4, ProjectID: 1, BucketID: 3}
    require.NoError(t, tb.Update(s, u))
    require.NoError(t, s.Commit())

    s = db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    stored := &TaskBucket{}
    has, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).Get(stored)
    require.NoError(t, err)
    require.True(t, has)
    require.Equal(t, int64(1), stored.BucketID, "recurring task should move to the To-Do/default bucket, not remain in Doing")
}

func (t *Task) moveTaskToDefaultBuckets(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, views []*ProjectView) error {
	for _, view := range views {
		bucketID, err := getDefaultBucketID(s, view)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		tb := &TaskBucket{
			BucketID:      bucketID,
			TaskID:        t.ID,
			ProjectViewID: view.ID,
			ProjectID:     t.ProjectID,
		}
		err = updateTaskBucket(s, a, tb)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		tp := TaskPosition{
			TaskID:        t.ID,
			ProjectViewID: view.ID,
			Position:      calculateDefaultPosition(t.Index, t.Position),
		}
		err = updateTaskPosition(s, a, &tp)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
	}
	return nil
}

  1506	func addRepeatIntervalToTime(now, t time.Time, duration time.Duration) time.Time {
  1507	        for {
  1508	                t = t.Add(duration)
  1509	                if t.After(now) {
  1510	                        break
  1511	                }
  1512	        }

		currentTaskBucket := &TaskBucket{}

		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		var bucketID = currentTaskBucket.BucketID

		// Task done, but no done bucket? Do nothing
		if t.Done && view.DoneBucketID == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Task not done, currently not in done bucket? Do nothing
		if !t.Done && bucketID != view.DoneBucketID {
			continue

		// Task done? Done bucket

func (t *Task) moveTaskToDefaultBuckets(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, views []*ProjectView) error {
	for _, view := range views {
		bucketID, err := getDefaultBucketID(s, view)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		err = t.moveTaskToBucket(s, a, view, bucketID)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
	}
	return nil
}

func (t *Task) moveTaskToBucket(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, view *ProjectView, bucketID int64) error {
	tb := &TaskBucket{
		BucketID:      bucketID,
		TaskID:        t.ID,
		ProjectViewID: view.ID,
		ProjectID:     t.ProjectID,
	}
	err := updateTaskBucket(s, a, tb)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	tp := TaskPosition{
		TaskID:        t.ID,
		ProjectViewID: view.ID,
		Position:      calculateDefaultPosition(t.Index, t.Position),
	}
	return updateTaskPosition(s, a, &tp)
}

package models

import (
    "testing"

    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/db"
    "code.vikunja.io/api/pkg/user"
    "github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func TestReproRecurringTaskMarkedDoneFromDoingMovesToTodo(t *testing.T) {
    db.LoadAndAssertFixtures(t)
    s := db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    u := &user.User{ID: 1}

    // Simulate the reproduction steps: recurring task is in Doing.
    _, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).
        Cols("bucket_id").
        Update(&TaskBucket{BucketID: 2})
    require.NoError(t, err)

    // User clicks "mark completed" in the task.
    task := &Task{ID: 28, Done: true, RepeatAfter: 3600}
    require.NoError(t, task.Update(s, u))
    require.NoError(t, s.Commit())

    s = db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    stored := &TaskBucket{}
    has, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).Get(stored)
    require.NoError(t, err)
    require.True(t, has)
    require.False(t, task.Done)
    require.Equal(t, int64(1), stored.BucketID, "recurring task should move to the To-Do/default bucket, not remain in Doing")
}

func TestReproRecurringTaskDraggedDoneFromDoingMovesToTodo(t *testing.T) {
    db.LoadAndAssertFixtures(t)
    s := db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    u := &user.User{ID: 1}

    _, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).
        Cols("bucket_id").
        Update(&TaskBucket{BucketID: 2})
    require.NoError(t, err)

    tb := &TaskBucket{TaskID: 28, ProjectViewID: 4, ProjectID: 1, BucketID: 3}
    require.NoError(t, tb.Update(s, u))
    require.NoError(t, s.Commit())

    s = db.NewSession()
    defer s.Close()
    stored := &TaskBucket{}
    has, err := s.Where("task_id = ? AND project_view_id = ?", 28, 4).Get(stored)
    require.NoError(t, err)
    require.True(t, has)
    require.Equal(t, int64(1), stored.BucketID, "recurring task should move to the To-Do/default bucket, not remain in Doing")
}
EOF

+func (t *Task) moveTaskToBucket(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, view *ProjectView, bucketID int64) error {
+	tb := &TaskBucket{
+		BucketID:      bucketID,
+		TaskID:        t.ID,
+		ProjectViewID: view.ID,
+		ProjectID:     t.ProjectID,
+	}
+	err := updateTaskBucket(s, a, tb)
+	if err != nil {
+		return err
+	}
+
+	tp := TaskPosition{
+		TaskID:        t.ID,
+		ProjectViewID: view.ID,
+		Position:      calculateDefaultPosition(t.Index, t.Position),
+	}
+	return updateTaskPosition(s, a, &tp)
+}

 func addOneMonthToDate(d time.Time) time.Time {
 	return time.Date(d.Year(), d.Month()+1, d.Day(), d.Hour(), d.Minute(), d.Second(), d.Nanosecond(), config.GetTimeZone())
 }

+func (t *Task) moveTaskToBucket(s *xorm.Session, a web.Auth, view *ProjectView, bucketID int64) error {

+		BucketID:      bucketID,

+		ProjectViewID: view.ID,
+		Position:      calculateDefaultPosition(t.Index, t.Position),
+	}
+	return updateTaskPosition(s, a, &tp)
